< text>
Food taste super good. Price are reasonable. Odor inside the restaurant are neutral doesn't smell good nor stink. The restaurant and grocery store are in a same big room divided into two. The restaurant are located close to a big intersection which is Blackstone and Herndon Ave. From a 5 stars review I would rate the restaurant between 4.0-4.7.</text>

My sisters and i just had one of the best spicy tofu soup there. You will never know how great spicy tofu soup is until you have theirs. It is a family restaurant with only the parents working there, so there will be some wait but they usually have the Korean tv show on for entertainment while you wait. < Review>
Ive been there three times in one week,.. well twice as they were closed on Tuesday afternoon.  Cakes are delicate, but the Almond Croissant is mind blowing.  The Chocolate Croissant probably is too, I loved it, but was happily distracted from the Almond I ate first.  I wouldn't usually eat two in a row, one was for my partner, but the egg sandwiches I picked up at another restaurant messed up my order,.. I said "no meat, just egg and cheese, and when I got home it was just meat, no egg or cheese.  I don't eat meat, so my partner ate it and gave me his croissant.  Long story short, The Chocolate Bar must be visited at least two or three times to maintain perspective on first impressions. The key is being selective, not over doing it. Do you get what I'm saying,.. the Almond was so good, that what I really needed was to be alone with the experience.  I will return most definitely, but it will always be an exercise in moderation.  Full disclosure, if it's baked and done well, I'm there.  Just in case you thought I was over selling.< /Review>

< text>
We ended up eating at Hurley's by happenstance. (The 2 restaurants to which we were recommended to go to, both had  2 hour waits) We could not have been happier, Christian our server was extremely accommodating and we were all pleasantly surprised by how delicious everything was. We had the calamari, Moroccan beef skewers and Atlantic mussels as appetizers. I had the short ribs as did my friend and it was melt in your mouth delicious. I have to say what a great surprise this place was, no bottle charge and the chocolate cake to top it all off was perfect. I highly recommend it!< /text>

<Review>My wife and I went to Napa for our 20th Anniversary. Hurley's was one of the establishments we visited (9/26/2015). The area and the atmosphere are very nice. The restaurant itself is pretty cool - decor, layout, etc, etc,. We expected the place to be on the pricey side, so, no problems there. The problem comes where you expect to get what you pay for. The value was just not there at this establishment. The server was a bit disheveled, although surprising for a restaurant like this, that's easily overlooked for a number of reasons - people can have bad days. Where my one star rating comes from was the "Seared Ahi". My wife and I love this dish and have enjoyed it countless times at a number of different establishments. It's pricey because it is Sushi grade fish that requires extra care to keep, prepare and present in order for it to be enjoyed properly (and without getting sick).

The Seared Ahi we were delivered was warm in the center (as opposed to cool). When searing cold Ahi Tuna properly, it is a very quick process that leaves the center of the fish cool. Additionally, the Ahi was served on a warm plate. Warm!. No, No, No... Never.. So what you have is warm raw fish being served on a warm plate - this is something that can turn bad almost immediately in these conditions. They're taking a premium dish and turning it into garbage and a health risk. I alerted the server to our surprise and borderline disgust immediately and asked her to consult the chef regarding this (because NO chef worth their salt is serving this dish this way).

Later, the manager came by the table to ask how everything was, well, we brought this to her attention and she said that she had consulted with the chef and that the dish was indeed served how the chef had intended. In total disbelief, I asked to consult with the chef. The manager said that they had JUST gone home (with a deer in the headlights look on her face). Mind you, it was 7pm, the height of the dinner hour - the place was filling up; ain't no way the chef is going home. She lied to me. No apologies or offer to make things right or anything like that - why would there be?, after all, it was the intention of the chef to serve fish on the fast track to decay and becoming scrombroidal - right?

We spoke with the server once again when paying the bill, because, it was she, Queen Of Dishevel, that stated she would speak with the chef. She didn't of course. She spoke with the manager. That's what they always do in hopes that the manager can provide some type of mechanism (which she made zero attempt to do) to keep their tip from being affected.

So, in essence, nobody cared that they were serving garbage, with health hazard risks, at a premium price.

In a nutshell, the issue was a chef that seemed ignorant to the dish, a manager that didn't care and a server that woke up ten minutes before coming to work.< /Review>< pictures>
None< /pictures>

I want to say thank you to everyone at CSLS especially Alyssa Ramirez.She was there from the first day I walked into the Van Nuys location to filling out the final paperwork to submit to the CSLB after passing both exams (on the first try). She was always available to answer any questions I had and  advise me of what I needed every step of the way. Alyssa, Thank you again!!
All the instructors were very knowledgeable and presented the information in an easy to understand format that was very similar to the format of the state exams.
All the study material was spot on. Very well organized and a great balance of text and audio. All the tests in the books were great study material in the 3 or 4 days prior to taking the exams.
I completed and passed the law section of the exam in just under an hour and the General B exam in just over an hour and a half. If it wasn't for CSLS, their amazing staff, and the way the study material is laid out I don't think I would have been able to breeze thru both exams the way that I did.

Thank you again to everyone at CSLS
Craig Toeller<//text>

< Text>
It looks like just an ordinary liquor store if you pass by, but if that's what you do, pass by, you'll have missed downtown's best sandwich shop.

You may note the Boar's Head logo signifying quality meats are used. That's just the beginning. The big assortment of freshly baked breads (try the rosemary roll) makes an even bigger difference. The salads are bomb too. All this comes with neighborly customer service, and a wine and premium liquor selection that will delight the most discriminating connoisseurs.

So glad I found this place!< /Text>

The owner was so kind, accommodating, and caring. This was one of the few places that had a reasonably priced vegetarian option for my friend. She got one of the vegetarian sandwiches and LOVED it! I got the G&H special and got one half toasted and one cold so I could eat it later and it was DELICIOUS both ways (but definitely recommend it hot.) I also got the pasta salad and it was very tasty. The owner was very patient with me and checked on us multiple times while we were there. You can tell he genuinely cares about his store, the quality of the food, and his customers. I highly recommend this place!!</text>

< Review>
If only I lived closer to this place, would definitely be going here more often. They just recently opened in the last few months and glad they did. It's a nice local deli with a delicious selection of freshly made sandwiches featuring Boarheads meat. The honey bee sandwich was perfect with turkey, bacon, avocado and a tangy mustard sauce. There are a few tables outside to eat or could  grab a sandwich to go and sit nearby at the park. The spot has broad selection of products that they sell like drinks, snacks, alcohol, etc... The gentlemen who helped us was friendly and personable, providing recommendations and making sure we were all set. It feels like it will become a local favorite in no time.</Review>
